# Awesome Elixir [![CI Badge](https://github.com/correia-jpv/fucking-awesome-elixir/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg)](https://github.com/correia-jpv/fucking-awesome-elixir) [![Awesome](https://cdn.rawgit.com/sindresorhus/awesome/d7305f38d29fed78fa85652e3a63e154dd8e8829/media/badge.svg)](https://github.com/sindresorhus/awesome)
A curated list of amazingly awesome Elixir libraries, resources, and shiny things inspired by <b><code>&nbsp;32054‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;5134üç¥</code></b> [awesome-php](https://github.com/ziadoz/awesome-php)).

If you think a package should be added, please add a :+1: (`:+1:`) at the according issue or create a new one.

There are [other sites with curated lists of elixir packages](#other-awesome-lists) which you can have a look at.

## Actors
*Libraries and tools for working with actors and such.*
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;210‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;6üç¥</code></b> [alf](https://github.com/antonmi/ALF)) - Flow-based Application Layer Framework.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;276‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;66üç¥</code></b> [bpe](https://github.com/spawnproc/bpe)) - Business Process Engine in Erlang.  üåé [Doc](bpe.n2o.dev)).
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;312‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;85üç¥</code></b> [pooler](https://github.com/seth/pooler)) - An OTP Process Pool Application.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;79‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;7üç¥</code></b> [poolex](https://github.com/general-CbIC/poolex)) - Pure elixir pool manager.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;338‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;13üç¥</code></b> [spawn](https://github.com/eigr/spawn)) - Elixir poliglot actors service mesh.

## Algorithms and Data structures
*Libraries and implementations of algorithms and data structures.*

* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;218‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;6üç¥</code></b> [aja](https://github.com/sabiwara/aja)) - High performance persistent vectors and ordered maps.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;36‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;8üç¥</code></b> [array](https://github.com/takscape/elixir-array)) - An Elixir wrapper library for Erlang's array.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;40‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3üç¥</code></b> [aruspex](https://github.com/dkendal/aruspex)) - Aruspex is a configurable constraint solver, written purely in Elixir.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;34‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3üç¥</code></b> [bimap](https://github.com/mkaput/elixir-bimap)) - Pure Elixir implementation of üåé [bidirectional maps](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bidirectional_map) and multimaps.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;36‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5üç¥</code></b> [bitmap](https://github.com/hashd/bitmap-elixir)) - Pure Elixir implementation of üåé [bitmaps](en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bitmap).
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;54‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;12üç¥</code></b> [blocking_queue](https://github.com/joekain/BlockingQueue)) - BlockingQueue is a simple queue implemented as a GenServer. It has a fixed maximum length established when it is created.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;112‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;8üç¥</code></b> [bloomex](https://github.com/gmcabrita/bloomex)) - A pure Elixir implementation of Scalable Bloom Filters.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;22‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2üç¥</code></b> [clope](https://github.com/ayrat555/clope)) - Elixir implementation of CLOPE: A Fast and Effective Clustering Algorithm for Transactional Data.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;37‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;11üç¥</code></b> [Closure Table](https://github.com/florinpatrascu/closure_table)) - Closure Table for Elixir - a simple solution for storing and manipulating complex hierarchies. It provides in-memory and Ecto adapters.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;34‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1üç¥</code></b> [combination](https://github.com/seantanly/elixir-combination)) - Elixir library to generate combinations and permutations from Enumerable collection.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;55‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3üç¥</code></b> [conrex](https://github.com/NAISorg/conrex)) - An Elixir implementation of the CONREC algorithm for topographic or isochrone maps.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;0üç¥</code></b> [count_buffer](https://github.com/camshaft/count_buffer)) - Buffer a large set of counters and flush periodically.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;42‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;0üç¥</code></b> [cuckoo](https://github.com/gmcabrita/cuckoo)) - A pure Elixir implementation of üåé [Cuckoo Filters](www.cs.cmu.edu/%7Edga/papers/cuckoo-conext2014.pdf).
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;55‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;6üç¥</code></b> [cuid](https://github.com/duailibe/cuid)) - Collision-resistant ids optimized for horizontal scaling and sequential lookup performance, written in Elixir.
* üåé [data_morph](hex.pm/packages/data_morph) - Create Elixir structs from data.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;63‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;7üç¥</code></b> [dataframe](https://github.com/JordiPolo/dataframe)) - Package providing functionality similar to Python's Pandas or R's data.frame().
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;218‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;19üç¥</code></b> [datastructures](https://github.com/meh/elixir-datastructures)) - A collection of protocols, implementations and wrappers to work with data structures.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;33‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5üç¥</code></b> [def_memo](https://github.com/os6sense/DefMemo)) - A memoization macro (defmemo) for elixir using a genserver backing store.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;0üç¥</code></b> [dlist](https://github.com/stocks29/dlist)) - Deque implementations in Elixir.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;34‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;6üç¥</code></b> [eastar](https://github.com/herenowcoder/eastar)) - A* graph pathfinding in pure Elixir.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;64‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;18üç¥</code></b> [ecto_materialized_path](https://github.com/asiniy/ecto_materialized_path)) - Tree structure, hierarchy and ancestry for the ecto models.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;100‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;20üç¥</code></b> [ecto_state_machine](https://github.com/asiniy/ecto_state_machine)) - Finite state machine pattern implemented on Elixir and  adopted for Ecto.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;19‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;0üç¥</code></b> [elistrix](https://github.com/tobz/elistrix)) - A latency / fault tolerance library to help isolate your applications from an uncertain world of slow or failed services.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;112‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5üç¥</code></b> [emel](https://github.com/mrdimosthenis/emel)) - A simple and functional machine learning library written in elixir.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;160‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;35üç¥</code></b> [erlang-algorithms](https://github.com/aggelgian/erlang-algorithms)) - Implementations of popular data structures and algorithms.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;290‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;20üç¥</code></b> [exconstructor](https://github.com/appcues/exconstructor)) - An Elixir library for generating struct constructors that handle external data with ease.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;11‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;6üç¥</code></b> [exfsm](https://github.com/awetzel/exfsm)) - Simple elixir library to define a static FSM.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;58‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;15üç¥</code></b> [exmatrix](https://github.com/a115/exmatrix)) - ExMatrix is a small library for working with matrices, originally developed for testing matrix multiplication in parallel.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;34‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3üç¥</code></b> [exor_filter](https://github.com/mpope9/exor_filter)) - Nif for xor_filters.  'Faster and Smaller Than Bloom and Cuckoo Filters'.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;0‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1üç¥</code></b> [ezcryptex](https://github.com/stocks29/ezcryptex)) - Thin layer on top of Cryptex.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1603‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;88üç¥</code></b> [flow](https://github.com/dashbitco/flow)) - Computational parallel flows on top of GenStage.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5üç¥</code></b> [fnv](https://github.com/asaaki/fnv.ex)) - Pure Elixir implementation of Fowler‚ÄìNoll‚ÄìVo hash functions.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;361‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;22üç¥</code></b> [fsm](https://github.com/sasa1977/fsm)) - Finite state machine as a functional data structure.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;510‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;52üç¥</code></b> [fuse](https://github.com/jlouis/fuse)) - This application implements a so-called circuit-breaker for Erlang.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;40‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3üç¥</code></b> [gen_fsm](https://github.com/pavlos/gen_fsm)) - A generic finite state-machine - Elixir wrapper around OTP's gen_fsm.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;12‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1üç¥</code></b> [graphex](https://github.com/stocks29/graphex)) - A library for composing and executing task graphs in elixir.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;87‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;13üç¥</code></b> [graphmath](https://github.com/crertel/graphmath)) - An Elixir library for performing 2D and 3D mathematics.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;24‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;18üç¥</code></b> [hash_ring_ex](https://github.com/reset/hash-ring-ex)) - A consistent hash-ring implementation for Elixir.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;20‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3üç¥</code></b> [hypex](https://github.com/whitfin/hypex)) - Fast Elixir implementation of HyperLogLog.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;20‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3üç¥</code></b> [indifferent](https://github.com/vic/indifferent)) - Indifferent access for Elixir maps/list/tuples with custom key conversion.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;4‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2üç¥</code></b> [isaac](https://github.com/arianvp/elixir-isaac)) - Isaac is an elixir module for ISAAC: a fast cryptographic random number generator.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;12‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2üç¥</code></b> [jumper](https://github.com/whitfin/jumper)) - Jump consistent hash implementation in Elixir (without NIFs).
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;7‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1üç¥</code></b> [key2value](https://github.com/okeuday/key2value)) - Erlang 2-way Set Associative Map.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;8‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;0üç¥</code></b> [lfsr](https://github.com/pma/lfsr)) - Elixir implementation of a binary Galois Linear Feedback Shift Register.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;225‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;14üç¥</code></b> [loom](https://github.com/asonge/loom)) - A CRDT library with Œ¥-CRDT support.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;17‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;12üç¥</code></b> [luhn](https://github.com/ma2gedev/luhn_ex)) - Luhn algorithm in Elixir.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;65‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;47üç¥</code></b> [lz4](https://github.com/szktty/erlang-lz4)) - LZ4 bindings for Erlang for fast data compressing.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;559‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;55üç¥</code></b> [machinery](https://github.com/joaomdmoura/machinery)) - A state machine library for structs in general, it integrates with Phoenix out of the box.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;12‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;0üç¥</code></b> [mason](https://github.com/spacepilots/mason)) - Coerce maps into structs. This is helpful e.g. when you interface a REST API and want to create a struct from the response.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;485‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;32üç¥</code></b> [matrex](https://github.com/versilov/matrex)) - A blazing fast matrix library for Elixir/Erlang with C implementation using CBLAS.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;96‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;16üç¥</code></b> [merkle_tree](https://github.com/yosriady/merkle_tree)) - A Merkle hash tree implementation in Elixir.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;4‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1üç¥</code></b> [minmaxlist](https://github.com/seantanly/elixir-minmaxlist)) - Elixir library extending `Enum.min_by/2`, `Enum.max_by/2` and `Enum.min_max_by/2` to return a list of results instead of just one.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;4‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;6üç¥</code></b> [mmath](https://github.com/dalmatinerdb/mmath)) - A library for performing math on number 'arrays' in binaries.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;307‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;12üç¥</code></b> [monadex](https://github.com/rob-brown/MonadEx)) - Upgrade your Elixir pipelines with monads.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;39‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;7üç¥</code></b> [murmur](https://github.com/gmcabrita/murmur)) - A pure Elixir implementation of the non-cryptographic hash Murmur3.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;18‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5üç¥</code></b> [nary_tree](https://github.com/medhiwidjaja/nary_tree)) - An Elixir implementation of generic n-ary tree data structure.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;14‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;6üç¥</code></b> [natural_sort](https://github.com/DanCouper/natural_sort)) - Elixir natural sort implementation for lists of strings.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;0üç¥</code></b> [navigation_tree](https://github.com/gutschilla/elixir-navigation-tree)) - A navigation tree representation with helpers to generate HTML out of it.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;103‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;19üç¥</code></b> [parallel_stream](https://github.com/beatrichartz/parallel_stream)) - A parallel stream implementation for Elixir.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;29‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3üç¥</code></b> [paratize](https://github.com/seantanly/elixir-paratize)) - Elixir library providing some handy parallel processing (execution) facilities that support configuring number of workers and timeout.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;64‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2üç¥</code></b> [parex](https://github.com/StevenJL/parex)) - Parallel Execute (Parex) is an Elixir module for executing multiple (slow) processes in parallel.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;6‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;0üç¥</code></b> [qcomplex](https://github.com/q60/complex)) - Elixir library implementing complex numbers and math operations for them.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;34‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5üç¥</code></b> [qex](https://github.com/princemaple/elixir-queue)) - Wraps `:queue`, with improved API and `Inspect`, `Collectable` and `Enumerable` protocol implementations.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;0üç¥</code></b> [qrational](https://github.com/q60/rational)) - Elixir library implementing rational numbers and math operations for them.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;42‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9üç¥</code></b> [ratio](https://github.com/Qqwy/elixir-rational)) - Adds Rational Numbers and allows them to be used in common arithmetic operations. Also supports conversion between Floats and Rational Numbers.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;37‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;14üç¥</code></b> [red_black_tree](https://github.com/SenecaSystems/red_black_tree)) - Red-Black tree implementation in Elixir.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;141‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;17üç¥</code></b> [remodel](https://github.com/stavro/remodel)) - An Elixir presenter package used to transform map structures.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3üç¥</code></b> [rendezvous](https://github.com/timdeputter/Rendezvous)) - Implementation of the Rendezvous or Highest Random Weight (HRW) hashing algorithm in Elixir.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;12‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;4üç¥</code></b> [rock](https://github.com/ayrat555/rock)) - Elixir implementation of ROCK: A Robust Clustering Algorithm for Categorical Attributes.

## Feature Flags and Toggles
*Libraries to manage feature toggles (AKA feature flags): ON/OFF values that can be toggled at runtime through some interface*

* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;21‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;4üç¥</code></b> [ConfigCat](https://github.com/configcat/elixir-sdk)) - Elixir SDK for ConfigCat hosted feature flag service.

* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1148‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;88üç¥</code></b> [fun_with_flags](https://github.com/tompave/fun_with_flags)) - A feature toggle library using Redis or Ecto for persistence, an ETS cache for speed and PubSub for distributed cache busting. Comes with a management web UI for Phoenix and Plug.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;77‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;3üç¥</code></b> [molasses](https://github.com/securingsincity/molasses)) - A feature toggle library using redis or SQL (using Ecto) as a backing service.

## Geolocation
*Libraries for geocoding addresses and working with latitudes and longitudes.*

* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;29‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;7üç¥</code></b> [distance_api_matrix](https://github.com/C404/distance-matrix-api)) - Provide distance and heading calculations via Google distance matrix api.

* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;29‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;11üç¥</code></b> [geohash](https://github.com/polmuz/elixir-geohash)) - Geohash encode/decode library.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;?‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;?üç¥</code></b> [geohash_nif](https://github.com/wstucco/geohash_nif/)) - Drop in replacement for Geohash encode/decode library implemented as a NIF.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;12‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;6üç¥</code></b> [geohax](https://github.com/evuez/geohax)) - Geohash encoding and decoding with neighbors finder.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;124‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;20üç¥</code></b> [geoip](https://github.com/navinpeiris/geoip)) - Find geolocation for a given IP, hostname or `Plug.Conn`.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;191‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;18üç¥</code></b> [geolix](https://github.com/mneudert/geolix)) - MaxMind GeoIP2 database reader/decoder.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;24‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;7üç¥</code></b> [geonames](https://github.com/pareeohnos/geonames-elixir)) - A simple Elixir wrapper around the GeoNames API.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;18‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1üç¥</code></b> [ip2location](https://github.com/nazipov/ip2location-elixir)) - An Elixir library for IP2Location database.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;7‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1üç¥</code></b> [ipgeobase](https://github.com/sergey-chechaev/elixir_ipgeobase)) - Find Russian and Ukraine city by IP address and find country for other country.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;6üç¥</code></b> [proj](https://github.com/CandyGumdrop/proj)) - Elixir coordinate conversion library using OSGeo's PROJ.4.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;7‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;1üç¥</code></b> [segseg](https://github.com/pkinney/segseg_ex)) - Segment-segment intersection classifier and calculator.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;7‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;0üç¥</code></b> [srtm](https://github.com/adriankumpf/srtm)) - Query locations for elevation data from the NASA Shuttle Radar Topography Mission.

## HTML
*Libraries and implementations working with HTML (for xml tools please go to the [XML](#xml) section).*

* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;2129‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;161üç¥</code></b> [floki](https://github.com/philss/floki)) - A simple HTML parser that enables searching using CSS like selectors.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;285‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;71üç¥</code></b> [html_sanitize_ex](https://github.com/rrrene/html_sanitize_ex)) - HTML sanitizer for Elixir.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;323‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;26üç¥</code></b> [meseeks](https://github.com/mischov/meeseeks#html)) - A library for parsing and extracting data from HTML and XML with CSS or XPath selectors.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;31‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5üç¥</code></b> [modest_ex](https://github.com/f34nk/modest_ex)) - A library to do pipeable transformations on html strings with CSS selectors, e.g. find(), prepend(), append(), replace() etc.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;14‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5üç¥</code></b> [myhtmlex](https://github.com/Overbryd/myhtmlex)) - Elixir/Erlang bindings for lexborisov's myhtml.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;279‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;60üç¥</code></b> [readability](https://github.com/keepcosmos/readability)) - Readability is for extracting and curating articles.
* üåé [texas](gitlab.com/dgmcguire/texas) - Texas is a powerful abstraction over updating your clients using server-side rendering and server-side Virtual DOM diff/patching.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;2üç¥</code></b> [tidy_ex](https://github.com/f34nk/tidy_ex)) - Elixir binding to the granddaddy of HTML tools [http://www.html-tidy.org](http://www.html-tidy.org).
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;57‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;0üç¥</code></b> [vnu-elixir](https://github.com/angelikatyborska/vnu-elixir)) - Elixir client for the üåé [Nu HTML Checker](validator.w3.org/nu/). Provides HTML, CSS, and SVG validation.

# Resources
Various resources, such as books, websites and articles, for improving your Elixir development skills and knowledge.

## Books
*Fantastic books and e-books.*

* üåé [Adopting Elixir](pragprog.com/book/tvmelixir/adopting-elixir) - Bring Elixir into your company, with real-life strategies from the people who built Elixir and use it successfully at scale. This book has all the information you need to take your application from concept to production (2017).
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;173‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;11üç¥</code></b> [Async Elixir](https://github.com/Arp-G/async-elixir)) - Dive into Elixir's world of concurrency and processes with this interactive Livebook.
* üåé [Craft GraphQL APIs in Elixir with Absinthe](pragprog.com/book/wwgraphql/craft-graphql-apis-in-elixir-with-absinthe) - Upgrade your web API to GraphQL, leveraging its flexible queries to empower your users, and its declarative structure to simplify your code (2017).
* üåé [Elixir Cookbook](www.packtpub.com/application-development/elixir-cookbook) - This book is a set of recipes grouped by topic by Paulo A Pereira (2015).
* üåé [Elixir do zero √† concorr√™ncia](www.casadocodigo.com.br/products/livro-elixir) - (Portuguese) The book provides introduction to functional and concurrent programming with Elixir by Tiago Davi (2014).
* üåé [Elixir in Action](www.manning.com/books/elixir-in-action) - A brief intro to the language followed by a more detailed look at building production-ready systems in Elixir by Sa≈°a Juriƒá (2015).
* üåé [Elixir in Action, Second Edition](www.manning.com/books/elixir-in-action-second-edition) - Revised and updated for Elixir 1.7, Elixir in Action, Second Edition teaches you how to apply Elixir to practical problems associated with scalability, fault tolerance, and high availability (2019).
* üåé [Elixir in Action, Third Edition](www.manning.com/books/elixir-in-action-third-edition) - Fully updated to Elixir 1.14, this authoritative bestseller reveals how Elixir tackles problems of scalability, fault tolerance, and high availability (2023).
* üåé [Elixir Succinctly](www.syncfusion.com/ebooks/elixir-succinctly) - A short book to learn the basic of Elixir and its ecosystem.
* üåé [Engineering Elixir Applications](pragprog.com/titles/beamops/engineering-elixir-applications/) - _(currently in Beta)_ As the subtitle suggests, this book explores the technologies and skills that support navigating each stage of software delivery with confidence.
* üåé [Erlang and Elixir for Imperative Programmers](leanpub.com/erlangandelixirforimperativeprogrammers) - Introduction to Erlang and Elixir in the context of functional concepts by Wolfgang Loder (2016).
* [Erlang in Anger](http://www.erlang-in-anger.com/) - This book intends to be a little guide about how to be the Erlang medic in a time of war by Fred Hebert (2014).
* üåé [Functional Web Development with Elixir, OTP, and Phoenix](pragprog.com/book/lhelph/functional-web-development-with-elixir-otp-and-phoenix) - Open doors to powerful new techniques that will get you thinking about web development in fundamentally new ways (2017).
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;101‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;4üç¥</code></b> [Getting Started - Elixir](https://github.com/potatogopher/elixir-getting-started)) - PDF, MOBI, and EPUB documents for Elixir's Getting Started tutorial (2016).
* üåé [Hands-on Elixir & OTP: Cryptocurrency trading bot](www.elixircryptobot.com) - Want to learn Elixir & OTP by creating a real-world project? With Hands-on *Elixir & OTP: Cryptocurrency trading bot* you will gain hands-on experience by working on an interesting software project. We will explore all the key abstractions and essential principles through iterative implementation improvements. (2021).
* [Introducing Elixir ](http://shop.oreilly.com/product/0636920030584.do) - A gentle introduction to the language, with lots of code examples and exercises by Simon St. Laurent and J. David Eisenberg (2013).
* üåé [Learn Functional Programming with Elixir](pragprog.com/book/cdc-elixir/learn-functional-programming-with-elixir) - Don‚Äôt board the Elixir train with an imperative mindset! To get the most out of functional languages, you need to think functionally (2017).
* üåé [Metaprogramming Elixir: Write Less Code, Get More Done (and Have Fun!)](pragprog.com/book/cmelixir/metaprogramming-elixir) - Thorough explanation on how to exploit Elixir's metaprogramming capabilities to improve your Elixir coding by Chris McCord (2015).
* [Phoenix for Rails Developers](http://www.phoenixforrailsdevelopers.com) - This book shows how Rails developers can benefit from their existing knowledge to learn Phoenix. By Elvio Vicosa (2017).
* üåé [Phoenix in Action](manning.com/books/phoenix-in-action) - builds on your existing web dev skills, teaching you the unique benefits of Phoenix along with just enough Elixir to get the job done. By Geoffrey Lessel (2017).
* üåé [Phoenix Inside Out](shankardevy.com/phoenix-book/) - The goal of this series is to enable you as a Confident Phoenix developer. There are 3 different editions to address varied needs of devs jumping into Phoenix.
* üåé [Programming Elixir 1.6](pragprog.com/titles/elixir16/) - The book provides introduction to functional and concurrent programming with Elixir by Dave Thomas (2014).
* üåé [Programming Phoenix 1.4](pragprog.com/titles/phoenix14/) - Definitive guide to build web applications with the Phoenix framework by Chris McCord, Jos√© Valim and Bruce Tate (2015).
* üåé [The Beam Book](happi.github.io/theBeamBook/) - A description of the Erlang Runtime System ERTS and the virtual Machine BEAM.
* üåé [The Little Elixir & OTP Guidebook](www.manning.com/books/the-little-elixir-and-otp-guidebook) - A book for learning Elixir and OTP through small to medium-sized projects by Benjamin Tan Wei Hao (2014).
* üåé [The Phoenix LiveView Cookbook](www.liveviewcookbook.com/) - A Phoenix LiveView e-book containing tried and tested recipes for solving common problems.
* üåé [√âtudes for Elixir](www.oreilly.com/library/view/etudes-for-elixir/9781491917640/) - A collection of exercises to program in Elixir by J. David Eisenberg (2013) (<b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;520‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;157üç¥</code></b> [Github Repo](https://github.com/oreillymedia/etudes-for-elixir))).

Implements the JSON-based "Language Server Protocol" standard and provides debugger support via VS Code's debugger protocol.

## Reading
*Elixir-related reading materials.*

* üåé [Discover Elixir & Phoenix](www.ludu.co/course/discover-elixir-phoenix/) - An online course that teaches both the Elixir language and the Phoenix framework.
* [Elixir Cheat-Sheet](http://media.pragprog.com/titles/elixir/ElixirCheat.pdf) - A Elixir cheat sheet, by Andy Hunt & Dave Thomas.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;1499‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;56üç¥</code></b> [Elixir Code Smells](https://github.com/lucasvegi/Elixir-Code-Smells)) - A catalog of Elixir-specific code smells that can harm the quality of software developed using this language.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;362‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;22üç¥</code></b> [Elixir Functional Programming](https://github.com/kblake/functional-programming)) - Material to introduce functional programming using the Elixir language.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;183‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;4üç¥</code></b> [Elixir Refactorings](https://github.com/lucasvegi/Elixir-Refactorings)) - A catalog of refactoring strategies to promote the redesign and improve the quality of code developed with Elixir.
* üåé [Elixir School](elixirschool.com/) - Lessons about the Elixir programming language.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;106‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9üç¥</code></b> [Elixir Tab](https://github.com/efexen/elixir-tab)) - Chrome Extension which helps you learn the Elixir core lib.
* üåé [Elixir vs Ruby | How Switching To Elixir Made Our Team Better](foxbox.com/blog/elixir-vs-ruby/) - Long-form post that explains in detail when and why you should choose Elixir over Ruby.
* üåé [Learn With Me: Elixir](inquisitivedeveloper.com/tag/lwm-elixir/) - A series where I learn Elixir and you can learn along with me.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;348‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;8üç¥</code></b> [The Little Schemer in Elixir](https://github.com/jwhiteman/a-little-elixir-goes-a-long-way)) - Exercises and algorithms from the Little Schemer book, ported to Elixir.
* <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;651‚≠ê</code></b> <b><code>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;405üç¥</code></b> [xElixir](https://github.com/exercism/xelixir)) - Exercism Exercises in Elixir.
